中常會決議國民大會延期舉行　俟各地代表選出卽行定期召集 21

The Central Standing Committee Decides to Postpone the National Assembly, to be Convened Regularly After Representatives from Various Places are Elected

(Nanjing) The Central Committee held its 23rd Standing Committee meeting at 9:00 AM on the 15th. More than 20 people attended, including Feng Yuxiang, Ye Chucang, Chen Lifu, Ding Weifen, Sun Ke, Ju Zheng, Zhou Fo Hai, Fang Zhi, Lin Sen, Zhang Ji, Zhang Lisheng, Chen Guofu, Shao Yuanchong and Zhou Qigang. Feng Yuxiang chaired the meeting, and the following important cases were resolved: (1) Regarding the case of how to deal with the fact that various provinces and cities failed to complete the National Assembly elections according to the original schedule, it was resolved that the National Assembly should be postponed because the election of representatives to the National Assembly has not been completed on schedule and in accordance with the law. Once the representatives from all over the country are elected in accordance with the law, they will be convened regularly. (2) Passed the public burial of Wu Xingya and Xu Shaozhen. (3) Appointed Zheng Peng as the Chief of the General Affairs Section of the Central Statistics Office. (4) Appointed Chen Bai as the Secretary of the Central Cultural Planning Committee. (5) Chen Guofu was elected as the chairman for the Central Memorial Week next Monday and reported. (6) Other routine cases. (Central News Agency telegram, 15th)

(Nanjing) The Central Standing Committee passed the postponement of the National Election on the 15th. According to Jiang Zuobin, whom reporters visited, only 17 provinces and cities reported the results of the preliminary election by the Double Ten Festival as originally scheduled. Some provinces and cities have not yet completed the oath registration of citizens. In view of the actual difficulties, the Central Government decided that it would be difficult to complete the elections by the original deadline, so it was decided to postpone them. This is neither a change of the previous agreement by the Central Government nor a request from various provinces. After the postponement, everything will proceed as usual, and the provinces and cities that have not yet completed the preliminary election will be urged to handle them in accordance with the law. After the preliminary elections in the provinces and cities are completed, the General Office of the National Election will submit a request to the Central Government for approval and send it back for the second election. According to my observation, it will take another three or four months to complete the election of representatives. The Central Government will then set the date of the meeting. The outside world's claim that the meeting will be postponed indefinitely is absolutely incorrect. (Central News Agency telegram, 15th)

(Nanjing) A member of the Central Committee said that the postponement of the National Assembly was decided by the Central Standing Committee due to actual needs. Since the establishment of the General Office of Elections, it has urged various provinces, cities, and professional groups to hold elections. Due to the vast territory and the lack of rapid local election organizations, only half of the regional and professional elections have been completed by the deadline of October 10 for the second election. Special elections are all pending. We must be cautious at the beginning. As for when the exhibition will be held, it will be determined by the speed of the election. At that time, the Central Standing Committee will make a decision based on the report submitted by the General Election Office. Whether the General Election Office will reduce the scope during the postponement of the conference will also be decided by the General Election Office after considering the situation and submitting it to the National Government for approval. The Central Standing Committee has not made a decision. (Special dispatch, 15th)

就業訓導班開學禮　丁惟汾報告設立宗旨及經過　翁文灝代表蔣院長宣讀訓詞 22

Opening Ceremony of the Employment Training Class, Ding Weifen Reports on the Purpose and Process of Establishment, Weng Wenhao Reads the Admonition on Behalf of President Chiang

(Nanjing) The opening ceremony of the Employment Training Class was held at the Central Political School at 10:00 AM on the 15th. Weng Wenhao, Ding Weifen, Wang Shijie, Wu Dingchang, Zhang Qun, Chen Shuren, Zhou Yawei, Chen Guofu, Lei Zhen, Zhang Lisheng, Liu Zhendong, and others, as representatives of President Chiang, as well as all the students and professors, totaling more than 400 people, attended. All faculty and students of the Central Political School and its four affiliated colleges attended the ceremony, totaling about 2,000 people. Ding Weifen presided over the ceremony and reported on the purpose of the establishment of the class and the preparation process. Weng Wenhao read the admonition on behalf of President Chiang, followed by Wang Shijie and Wu Dingchang giving admonitions. The ceremony ended with a group photo. (Central News Agency telegram, 15th)

The main idea of Wang Shijie's admonition is that the government is holding this class because it has seen two diseases in the lives of young people today: decadence and romance. Decadence is formed due to the lack of physical fitness and the inability to endure hardship, and romance is formed due to the lack of simplicity and heart rate. This class emphasizes physical training to promote physical health and spiritual training to improve living habits. I hope that all members will regard today's opening ceremony as the beginning of a new era in their new lives, so as not to fail the expectations of the country and society.

The main idea of Wu Dingchang's admonition is that at a time when national construction needs talents, there is unemployment. This is not only a loss for young people, but also a major loss for the government and society. The cause of national construction is progressing day by day, and those who are responsible for this advancement must first receive specialized training in order to be qualified. The purpose of this class is to be able to introduce and assign jobs to each member after graduation, so that everyone can make the best use of their talents. Only then can the mission of this class be said to be completed, otherwise young people will hardly be able to escape their responsibilities. I hope that everyone can abide by discipline, obey training, and complete the mission of this class. (Central News Agency telegram, 15th)

Chiang Kai-shek's Admonition

The Significance of Creation: The Essence of Education 23

(Nanjing) The Employment Training Class held its opening ceremony at the Central Political School on the morning of the 15th. President Chiang's address, entitled "The Significance of the Establishment of the Employment Training Class and the Essence of Education," was read by Weng Wen. The original text is as follows:

In order to enable graduates of colleges and above throughout the country to engage in appropriate work and make the greatest possible contributions, the Central Government has specially prepared the Employment Training Class, affiliated with the Central Political School, which officially opens today. In this time of national crisis, gathering so many university and college graduates and providing them with job preparation training is a pioneering initiative by the government to directly address the problem of youth unemployment. The purpose is not only to solve the livelihoods of individual scholars. Zhongzheng (Chiang Kai-shek) will elaborate on the significance of the establishment of this class and the essence of education, to inform all students of this class. Learning in youth is for the ability to act in adulthood; learning is originally intended for practical application. If learning cannot be applied, it is a waste of effort for the individual and a loss and burden to society. It will be seen that the more scholars there are, the more idlers there will be, the more difficult people's lives will be, and the weaker and more incurable the country will be. Today, Chinese youth often find that their knowledge is useless and they are often unemployed. They use their knowledge inappropriately and achieve little success, eventually leading to the contradictory phenomenon of everyone seeking work and every job needing people. This not only exposes the defects of education but also evolves into a serious social problem. The state establishes education to cultivate talent. If there is learning, there must be application. If supply and demand are not balanced, both the public and private sectors will suffer losses. There are many reasons why so many intellectuals in our country are unemployed. For example, economic poverty and the failure of various industries to thrive, the lack of reform in governance and the failure to appoint the virtuous and capable, and social chaos and the inability to distinguish between talent and foolishness are all objective reasons why learning is useless. The state should do its best to find ways to eliminate these causes. However, observing the facts, those young people who are truly talented, intelligent, and have practical learning are ultimately few in number who are suppressed and wasted. And the demand for talent in emerging public and private undertakings is expanding daily, yet there is nowhere where it is not felt that truly suitable candidates are difficult to find. Therefore, defects in education and the lack of sound self-cultivation among young people are also undeniable facts. The mismatch between talent and career is a subjective reason that urgently needs to be remedied. As the saying goes, "To fail to teach the people to fight is to abandon them." The state establishes education to cultivate citizens and, when they become talented, to enable them to contribute their abilities to complement the workings of heaven and human affairs, so as to achieve the purpose of opening up things and completing tasks. This matter is no different from war. If the government cannot fulfill its educational responsibilities and allows young people who are unprepared and lack sound self-cultivation to lightly enter society, ending their lives in frustration and failure, how can it not be considered abandonment? Therefore, Zhongzheng has long regarded the relief of unemployed youth as the government's top priority, believing that China is striving for national rejuvenation, the need for talent is great, and the approach should be rapid. The government cannot sit idly by and watch the disconnect between manpower and career without seeking a prompt remedy. The fundamental solution is to seek practicality and application in education at all levels, while the short-term solution is to address the shortcomings of young people themselves, providing short-term special training to remedy the shortcomings of their past schooling, and then allocating them to jobs that suit their individual personalities, cultivating their interest in employment and service, and adding assessment and promotion, and guiding them to make the greatest contribution. Although the beginning is simple, the hope is great. This step will be followed and continued, so that all young people in the country can have learning that is useful, and application that is suitable for their learning, so that everyone has a job and every job gets the right person. The significance of the establishment of this class lies in this, and the fundamental essence of education in this class can also be stated: (1) Practical ability must be enhanced. The common ailment of today's youth is that they like to talk about empty theories and lack the ability to do practical work. They emphasize rigid knowledge and neglect practical learning. Even if they have special and profound attainments in theory and book knowledge, they rarely have a deep understanding of ordinary physical and human affairs, and how the subjects they have learned can be combined with practical things, nor do they bother to humbly study them. They only know how to observe the superficial appearance of everything, but cannot deeply examine its actual content, so that as soon as they leave the classroom, they feel lost, and when they encounter practical problems, they often feel at a loss. The education of this class is primarily to remedy this shortcoming. Although the time is short, it is essential to provide practical training to students in each subject, to thoroughly integrate what they have learned, and to guide them on how to apply it, so that their working ability can adapt to the actual situation of their employment. General training should focus on enriching common knowledge and understanding human affairs and the physical world. It should also emphasize the order of priority in all things, the methods of managing people and things, and the appropriateness of adapting to time and place, so that practical ability can be enhanced and what has been learned can be applied. (2) The concept of employment should be corrected. In addition to the problem of youth unemployment today, there is also the problem of being unable to settle down in a job. They compare the amount of compensation and treatment, and only seek work that is simple and easy. The prevailing trend is that even a few ambitious people cannot escape the pursuit of individual interests. This is a sign of national decline, and must be corrected first. People are born into a group, and who does not take the resources for food, clothing, education, and upbringing from society? To have received, one must give. Of the vastness of China, those who have received university or specialized education are very few. If these very few intellectuals are only concerned with their own well-being, who will shoulder the heavy responsibility for the prosperity and decline of the nation and society? Even in terms of personal achievement, one cannot establish a life without establishing a life of service and devote oneself to the distant and great. All the heroes and outstanding figures of ancient and modern times, both Chinese and foreign, who have achieved virtue and established careers and are immortal, have all taken the hunger and drowning of the world as their own responsibility, sacrificing themselves and serving the people, starting from the single thought of benefiting others. Yu the Great wore coarse clothes and ate poorly, exhausting himself for the sake of the world. Mozi rubbed his head and touched his heels, practicing frugality. Buddha said, "If I don't go to hell, who will go to hell?" All of these are examples of embracing the great ambition of benefiting others and saving the world, and developing the spirit of service and sacrifice to complete their highest personality. Sun Yat-sen said, "Young people should aspire to do great things," and also said, "Life should be for the purpose of service." Zhongzheng has always adhered to Sun Yat-sen's teachings, explored the insights of past sages, and studied the true meaning of life, and has concluded that "the purpose of life is to improve the lives of all mankind, and the meaning of life is to create the life that succeeds the universe." I hope that all students in this class will understand the ultimate truth that righteousness and benefit are consistent, correct all selfish and self-serving concepts, and take saving the country and the world as the fundamental duty of scholars, so that entering the world to serve will have an active and upward interest, and there will be no worry of decline and waste. (3) The morality of service should be cultivated. The reason why public and private enterprises in our country are not prosperous is not only due to a lack of specialized talent, but also because those who are employed in general lack a deep understanding and habit of adhering to the morality of service. Therefore, the more people are employed by public and private institutions and organizations, the lower the efficiency. To mention the most obvious, such as respecting the system, obeying discipline, recognizing rights and responsibilities, cooperating and helping each other, and even cherishing public property, emphasizing timeliness, handling affairs meticulously, and being responsible in all matters, are all necessary conditions for the success of all undertakings. However, the more education today's youth receive, the farther their behavior and habits are from these service ethics. As a result, the general public regards employing knowledgeable youth as a difficult path, so how can it not create a large amount of unemployment? All of these phenomena have their social causes, but they are also a kind of defect in education that urgently needs to be remedied. Since this class is based on training and guidance for employment, the programs of service ethics must be clearly presented and students must be encouraged to practice them, so that those who are trained in this class will not be ashamed to be independent and striving members of the present era in any profession they take up in the future. They will be diligent and able to achieve something without supervision. The most important method for this training is to make the Twelve Rules of Conduct for Members of the Party the guiding principle, to show students the basics of dealing with the world and establishing themselves, and Zhongzheng's four words that he repeatedly reminds his comrades to "understand etiquette and righteousness, know integrity and shame, take responsibility, and abide by discipline," he sincerely hopes that the students will be familiar with them throughout their lives, embody them and strive to practice them. Confucius said, "To act with shame is the beginning of responsibility." To know the sorrow of the weakness and poverty of the nation, all of which is due to the failure of the people to strive, then one must bravely take responsibility and think about how to save it. With this in mind to serve, then how can there be a moment of procrastination, with this ambition to work, then one must be able to endure hard work and not refuse complaints. This is also the highest standard of service ethics. (4) Daily life must be reformed. Any great undertaking starts from the ordinary. There is no one who can be promising if their daily life is not orderly, their habits are not pure and good, and their spirit is not invigorated. Today's youth often lead romantic lives, are infected with corruption, and are mentally depressed, resulting in weak bodies, fragile minds, and a failure to cultivate morality and careers. They are procrastinating and lazy, and they are afraid of difficulties and seek temporary peace, eventually leading to evil extravagance and self-abandonment. Such people, even if they have received higher education and have considerable talent and intelligence, will ultimately not be able to contribute to society and the country. In order to remedy this shortcoming, this class will strictly manage all aspects of students' daily life, such as food, clothing, housing, and transportation, without being annoyed by trivial details, so that students can regulate their bodies and minds through the orderliness of their lives, and develop a solemn and respectful attitude. Then, all external temptations will not be able to enter. No matter what kind of career they take up, they will be able to persevere to the end and achieve final success. I hope that all students in this class will be able to consciously govern themselves, work hard and strive, and strictly abide by the six principles of "neatness," "cleanliness," "simplicity," "diligence," "promptness," and "thoroughness" in all their living habits, actions, and attitudes, so that their lives can be "militarized" and productive, so as to establish the foundation for their future achievement of virtue and career. We must fundamentally recognize that life is war, so we should be cautious and fearful at all times, and make every effort to face the enemy as if in battle. In short, there must be a arduous struggle, and then there will be a complete success. The reform of daily life is the basis of all morality. (5) Revolutionary faith must be established. Youth who live in today's China must recognize the mission of the era they bear if they want to make achievements. What is the mission of this era? It is to build the country through revolution and revive the Chinese nation. Sun Yat-sen's Three Principles of the People are the highest guiding principles and the only bright road for our complete revolution and the restoration of the nation. Therefore, our faith is concentrated on this, our will should be unified on this, our spirit should be united by this, and our strength should be developed by this. Only then can we unite thousands of young people into one person, unite the aspirations of thousands of people into one, and jointly shoulder the great mission of reviving the Chinese nation. The students must know that "to annex the weak and attack the disunited, to take advantage of chaos and insult the perishing" has been the case since ancient times, and it is even more so today. However, the cause of inviting insult must come from self-insult. There has never been a nation that was truly united and strong and ultimately insulted and destroyed by others. The emerging countries in the world at the beginning were not in distress and precarious, but only because their people could establish a revolutionary faith and, under the leadership of a single revolutionary doctrine and revolutionary government, struggled hard and never wavered, so that they could turn their country from danger to safety and from weakness to strength. With China's thick endowments, geographical advantages, cultural beauty, long history, and the greatness of the nation, if we do not destroy ourselves, who can destroy us? Once we are inspired, we will immediately revive. I hope that the students in this class will firmly believe in this belief, encourage themselves and encourage others, and the future of the country will be infinitely bright. (6) The spirit of self-reliance must be developed. There is one more most important meaning to tell the students, and that is self-reliance. The ancients discussed gentlemen, one said, "The gentleman strives for the root; when the root is established, the Way will come," another said, "The gentleman seeks in himself," and a third said, "Heaven's movement is ever vigorous; the gentleman strives for self-improvement without ceasing." The so-called "striving for the root" is self-cultivation. If a person can cultivate himself and illuminate his virtue, he can extend it to benefit the world, so it is said that "from the Son of Heaven to the common people, all regard self-cultivation as the root." If "the lazy cannot cultivate and the jealous fear others' cultivation," it is what the gentleman is most ashamed of. The so-called "seeking in oneself" is self-blame. The success or failure of a person's morality and career is all due to himself, and what can be relied on in the world is only oneself, so it is said, "Examine yourself first and blame others lightly," "Do not worry about not knowing, worry about not establishing," and "Do not ask about harvest, but ask about cultivation." The teachings of the past are all to encourage people to seek in themselves. "Striving for the root" is about things, "seeking in oneself" is about people, and the so-called "self-reliance" is about the fundamental spirit of these two. It is from this that the gentleman reflects on himself, inspires his will, cultivates virtue, and establishes a career. Only self-reliance has a positive and courageous spirit, only continuous efforts, only self-reliance has a great ambition of not admiring glory and profit, not greedy for enjoyment, not counting the gains and losses of the moment, and devoting oneself to achieving the greatest success in life. Zhongzheng sincerely hopes that the students will do their best to develop this spirit of "unceasing self-improvement," reflect on the progress or regress of their military morality and career at any time, strictly blame themselves, bravely renew themselves, and diligently cultivate themselves, so as to stand on their own feet and further establish others with self-reliance and save the country with self-rescue, then it will not only be the achievements of the students themselves, but also the benefit of the future of the country and society. The significance of the establishment of this class and the essence of education are roughly as described above. I hope that all the students who receive training will understand this meaning together, so that the education of this class can achieve a complete effect, and the students' morality and career will have the greatest success. When everyone does their best, the country will be revived. May the students strive! (Central News Agency dispatch on the 15th)

The Far East Anglo-Japanese-American Triangular Relationship (Part 1) 35

—To be translated

Soviet renowned political commentator Kantorovich published some years ago an authoritative work on the Far East problem, entitled "America in the Struggle for China among the Great Powers". (America in the Struggle for China) His sources for reference are extensive. Besides the daily newspapers and magazine articles about the history of America's relationship with the Far East, he referred to a number of materials from the never before published archives left behind by the Czarist government. In the final chapters of this book he made an analysis on the modern international Far East situation. After its publication, the author published several essays one after the other in Soviet publications exploring the state of affairs in this area. An American writer, Harriet Moore, has summarized this research by Kantorovich and has written it as a note, and it was published in the September edition of the Pacific Affairs quarterly. From this we can know roughly the kind of analysis that the Soviet scholar is making about the current state of affairs in the Far East. We now translate Moore's notes below:

The current situation in the Pacific is being controlled by a triangular relationship in policy among the powers of England, Japan and America. Although other countries are also involved, their influence is either comparatively unimportant or has a fixed nature that can be seen as a constant in an equation. Japan's policy of using military and economic methods to expand outward is also fixed, however the direction and speed of this expansion cannot help but be affected by the actions of the other two powers. Therefore, the state of affairs in the Pacific is actually determined by the changes in British and American policy. The fundamental goals of British and American policy are not changing. Both countries want to protect their current Far East interests, including those in China, both countries want to at least determine a suitable share for their own country in the rights of priority that can be obtained in the future in the Far East in business and investment. However, the strategies adopted in order to reach these goals, as well as the pressure coming from the deployed troops, are changing.

In 1931-32, at the beginning of Japan's invasion of Manchuria, the effective pressure of England and America decreased to almost nothing. The Anglo-American union that had been suppressing Japan at the Washington Conference had already disintegrated. The world's economic panic, England's abandoning the gold standard and the war debt problem deepened the contradictions between the two countries and impeded the cooperation between the two countries on the Far East front line. England does not fear its formidable rival Japan all that much. Commercial competition is still limited to a small number of industries. England's anti-Soviet emotions are very strong, hoping that Japan's expansion could be seen as a means to weaken the Soviet Union, and could also be used as a fortress to defend China from "revolution." The British colonies in the Pacific mostly opposed anti-Japan action because their trade with Japan was increasing, and their interests in China were minuscule; if Japan was only moving north, they would not encounter direct danger from the progress of Japan's invasion. Therefore, the policy that England was practicing was to take advantage of Japan's actions in order to push forward with its own anti-Soviet and anti-American attempts. England was playing this game of putting Japan and America on a scale to see who was lighter and who was heavier.

At the same time, America was practicing its traditional plan: doing its best to use "moral pressure" to protect itself. The flourishing of Stimson's "non-recognition" doctrine, protesting Japan's actions, cooperation with the League of Nations in the Lytton Commission and in its later verbal opposition to Japan's expansion: these were the limits of America's actions. America had also fallen into an economic panic, and was concentrating its attention on that. Its military equipment was very sparse, and due to Hoover's economic plan, it was impossible to start on even the steps of improvement. America's unilateral moral pressure was clearly not very effective, it only obtained international non-recognition of Japan's new position, and delayed the problem. England was unwilling to help, America had not recognized the Soviet Union, and China, because America was still hoping that Nanjing would exert its strength, was not prepared to cooperate effectively in any way. Therefore, America endured a vexation caused by "on paper" opposing Japan, and did not receive any results.

In the following two years, following the changes in world affairs, the positions of the two countries shifted. England's feeling of fear towards Japan grew. The commercial war expanded to new markets and new categories of goods. The "interlude" in Shanghai, due to the temporary union of China, England and America, although was a defeat for Japan, also eliminated the illusion that England and its colonies had been holding, that Japan's attempts were only focused on Northern China. The abrogation of the Washington Treaty caused the world military arms competition to repeat itself. Due to the deepening aggressiveness shown by Germany in all aspects, and Italy's adventure in Abyssinia, the European situation became even more tense. The increasing strength of the Soviet Union gradually pushed England's anti-Soviet nature behind the scenes. That the Soviet Union was a great latent force in the aspect of European stability, and that England had to win it over, became the obvious situation. And because the Soviet Union had become stronger, Japan had lost the certainty of being able to attack the Soviet Union in the near future. Thereupon Japan turned southward, and was infringing upon England's genuine interests.

A Record of an Interview with Shi Jianqiao: Feeling Uneasy Upon Hearing of the Pardon, Having Served Only Thirty-Six Days in Prison 36

(Tianjin) Shi Jianqiao's pardon order has not yet arrived in Tianjin. Officials say it is due to procedural matters and will take two weeks to arrive. According to her, her cousin Dong Shaofang visited her this morning and showed her a newspaper report about the pardon. She felt quite surprised. She had already been sentenced to seven years by the High Court and had given up hope of being spared. She reads and writes every day, planning to spend these seven years in sorrow. Now, being pardoned, she feels lost and vulnerable. It is noted that Shi was sent to the court for detention on November 14th of last year, undergoing seven trials. The Judicial Yuan Explains Various Doubts 43

(Nanjing) The Judicial Yuan explained the doubts about whether the wronged person can file a private prosecution in cases of perjury and false accusations. The crime of false accusation requires the intention to cause others to be subject to criminal or disciplinary punishment as a constituent element, and has the intention to infringe on personal legal interests while infringing on national legal interests. The falsely accused person can file a private prosecution. The constitution of the crime of perjury is different from the essential companion of the crime of false accusation, and of course no private prosecution can be filed. (15th Central News Agency Telegram)

Current Commentary

Sino-British Credit Loan and the Use of Foreign Capital 50

— Li

We still remember June 21st. Sir Frederick Leith-Ross, the British economic envoy to China, said while hosting reporters in Shanghai: British manufacturers and exporters should discuss with Chinese banks and government authorities about investing in credit to assist China in carrying out construction plans, so that China becomes increasingly prosperous, and the beneficiaries will not only be Britain, but all countries in the world will benefit. After Sir Frederick returned to his country, he actively campaigned in the British government and public circles based on this belief. After several months of efforts, the Sino-British credit loan agreement was finally established recently. Britain will lend China £10 million in credit, and China will be able to purchase large quantities of British goods under the guarantee of the British government. The method is the same as that stipulated in the British-Soviet Russian credit loan of £10 million in July of this year. The contents of the agreement have not yet been published, but the main points of the British-Soviet Russian commercial loan agreement established in July are: a term of ten years, an annual interest rate of 5.5%, and the issuance of loan certificates by the Soviet Russia to circulate in the London market, guaranteeing the repayment of the loan within a certain period. Taking this as an example, it is not difficult to see the outline of the agreement.

International credit loans are very common. The amount of this loan is not huge, but the process of its brewing has been more than a year. In March of last year, the British government proposed that, in accordance with the Nine-Power Treaty and the 1920 International Banking Consortium Agreement, countries should gather their strength to lend to China to assist in construction. This did not proceed due to Japanese opposition. In April, Britain proposed holding a conference in Nanjing to discuss China's monetary system, inviting representatives of banks from Japan, the United States, France, Belgium, and other countries to participate. This also failed to materialize due to Japan's disagreement. Later, Britain sent Sir Frederick Leith-Ross to China to investigate China's economic situation. During this period, Sir Frederick went to Japan twice to propose joint investment in China to the Japanese authorities, but was still not accepted by Japan. Since Britain's proposal has been repeatedly rejected by Japan, it will naturally invest in China alone to implement its beliefs.

After the news of the establishment of the Sino-British credit loan came out, there was a violent reaction in Tokyo. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs instructed its ambassador to Britain, Yoshida, to investigate the truth and prepare countermeasures. Political figures also stated that although Japan did not want to oppose construction loans used to promote China's revitalization, any loans containing political nature that could disrupt the peace and tranquility of East Asia would not be ignored by Japan and would not be protested. We do not want to criticize this kind of view, but we hope to point out that Britain's motive for lending to China this time is that in recent years, Britain's market in China has felt a great threat, and recently, the flooding of smuggled goods in North China has harmed Britain's legitimate trade. In order to maintain its market in China and promote its surplus goods, it had to find another way. Lending to China is the way it has found. And China happened to be in a time of economic construction and was actively proceeding, and of course it was very in need of foreign credit loans.

The use of foreign capital, on the surface, has no so-called good or evil. Egypt used foreign capital and therefore perished. The Soviet Union used foreign capital, but therefore completed construction. The success or failure between them does not lie in the use of foreign capital itself, but in the method of using foreign capital. China has a history of using foreign capital for forty years. Most of it was not used in productive enterprises, and even if a small number was used in productive enterprises, the principles of equality and mutual benefit were not strictly adhered to. Therefore, not only did we not get the benefits of using foreign capital, but we lost many sovereign rights. Although the use of foreign capital has become China's inevitable destiny in the future, how to use foreign capital is exactly the question that should be considered at present. According to the current situation and past historical experience, we believe that the use of foreign capital should at least adhere to the principles of equality and mutual benefit, and be absolutely limited to the productive sector.

Signs of Policy Changes in Belgium 51

(Brussels) Political figures here explained the speech made by King Leopold II, saying that its purpose was to express that the country's diplomatic policy and international status will be changed. In the future, Belgium's situation will be the same as before the war. In other words, the tasks Belgium bears will only be limited to guaranteeing its own territory, and not maintaining alliances with other countries, so as to avoid promoting international conflicts. For this reason, Belgium does not want to maintain the Franco-Belgian alliance, nor does it want to participate in the new Locarno Conference. According to reports, the opinions put forward by the King in this speech have been revealed in the previous speeches of Prime Minister Zeeland and Foreign Minister Spaak, and public opinion has long been prepared. Finally, the King officially announced it. It is found that the Flemish nationality in Belgium has always advocated an independent policy in diplomacy, and this nationality has recently occupied a considerable force in politics, which is probably the reason for the sudden change in this country's diplomatic policy. (14th Havas Telegram)

The Belgian King Announces Neutrality, European Situation Changes Greatly, Belgium Decides to Strengthen Military Force to Defend Itself, Averting Being Drawn into the Vortex of War 52

(Brussels) The King presided over the plenary session of the cabinet today, which was his first since he ascended the throne on February 23, 1934. The King spoke at the meeting, advocating that the country restore its pre-war neutrality policy. It is said that this policy must firmly place Belgium outside the wars of its neighbors, and must have sufficient strength to defend Belgium from any war. The commendable actions of the Netherlands and Switzerland are worthy of emulation, and it is stated that this is solely for the purpose of protecting Belgium from any war that may occur, and that Belgium's army system must be reorganized. Belgium's current military organization is no longer able to cope with the new possibility of the enemy's rapid entry, and this shortcoming should be remedied urgently. According to a Reuters correspondent in Paris, French political circles were not surprised by the King's remarks. French Foreign Minister Daladier had a long talk with the Belgian ambassador yesterday, and the ambassador must have informed Daladier of Belgium's decision. However, everyone feels that this decision has far-reaching implications and will be related to any new Locarno agreement, and must be carefully studied before opinions can be expressed. Although the military staff departments of France and Belgium have closely cooperated to plan defense, the two countries have not signed a defense alliance. (15th Reuters Telegram)

(London) The King's speech at the cabinet meeting, strongly advocating the restoration of Belgium's pre-war neutrality policy, has shocked the governments of European countries because this proposal has created a new political and military situation. Geneva regards this as a complete redefinition of Belgium's foreign policy. Although Belgium's remarks about the League of Nations should not be regarded as implying that Belgium's enthusiasm for supporting the League of Nations has weakened, everyone regards it as an obvious admission of the League of Nations' failure. There is also one thing that is particularly clear, that is, Belgium is no longer responsible for guaranteeing the territorial integrity and political independence of other countries. The King's declaration is tantamount to cancelling the Locarno Pact and the Franco-Belgian military agreement of 1920. Everyone believes that Belgium is deeply afraid of the unpredictable changes in the Franco-Soviet Russian Mutual Assistance Treaty, so it seeks to untie its guarantee on the Franco-German border. Now it is felt that a meeting of the signatory countries of the Locarno Pact, namely Britain, Germany, Belgium, France, and Italy, is all the more necessary as soon as possible, but Belgium's current attitude will make it necessary to greatly modify the basis for discussion. The King's speech was like a bolt from the blue. French newspapers have made passionate cries because they all believe that it is enough to greatly damage the hope of establishing a new Locarno Pact. The famous French commentator Bertinaux said that Belgium has now erased itself in the security chapter of international affairs, and has freed itself from the shackles of international treaties without consulting any country. The general public's reaction to the King's speech is full of deep concern, because the Franco-Belgian alliance has long been an important factor in France's national defense preparations. Now, due to Belgium's actions, the Maginot Line must be extended from the Belgian border to the coast. Berlin is also paying close attention to the King's remarks. The Berlin Daily said that this is fundamentally related to Belgium's future diplomatic and military policies. In addition, there are no other comments yet. Paris said that even if this country strictly adheres to its new policy of neutrality and withdraws from the League of Nations, the obligation to allow any army to pass through the Belgian territory will still be valid for two years. A Reuters diplomatic correspondent said that, from the perspective of British and French security, Belgium's return to neutral status is a major blow to both countries. If Belgium strictly adheres to neutrality, then the talks between the staff departments of Britain, France, and Belgium under the new Locarno Pact will be impossible. If a war breaks out in Europe, British and French aircraft cannot fly over Belgium, otherwise it will obviously be a violation of Belgium's neutrality. Britain and France will also lose the benefit of using Belgian air force bases as a stable reconnaissance post in emergencies. (15th Reuters Telegram)

The Belgian Cabinet Meeting Decides to Extend Military Service 53

(Brussels) The cabinet held a state meeting this morning, chaired by King Leopold III. It has been two and a half years since the King ascended the throne on, but today was the first time he chaired a state meeting. The government's draft military service bill was approved. This bill will be submitted for discussion at a special session of Parliament on the 27th of this month. Its content advocates that the term of service for infantry should be increased from sixteen months to eighteen months, and the term of service for artillery and engineering corps should be increased from eight months to twelve months. The King then gave an important speech, the main points of which are that Belgium must strengthen its national defense and become strong, so that neighboring countries will be deterred from invading Belgium or attacking third countries through this territory. Only then can Belgium engage in effective cooperation for peace in Western Europe and win the respect of peace-loving countries. Once something happens, various countries can also provide assistance to Belgium, especially since the obligations that Belgium bears in the international community should be limited to this, and it is unwilling to bear other obligations. The King then explained the reasons for Belgium's strengthening of national defense as follows: (1) Germany is reorganizing its military without sparing any effort. Italy and the Soviet Union have also been completely militarized. Even countries that love peace the most, such as Switzerland, have also begun to strengthen their national defense. Therefore, Belgium should take special measures to adapt to this situation. (2) Modern tactics are developing rapidly. This poses a greater threat to small countries like Belgium than to other countries. (3) After Germany re-established defenses along the Rhine River, the border line there has become the base for the country's future acts of aggression. (4) International treaties have been repeatedly violated in recent years, and even those freely signed by various countries have not been spared. As a result, the international security mechanism has been weakened. (5) Internal strife in a certain country has had repercussions internationally, and there is a risk of causing an unprecedented catastrophe. Based on the above reasons, Belgium has its own necessity to strengthen national defense. The purpose of the military policy adopted by Belgium is to prevent war, and not to conclude alliances with other countries in order to prepare for a victorious war. Since Germany abolished the Locarno Pact and re-established defenses along the Rhine River, Belgium's international position has almost returned to its original state before 1914. Now, to ensure Belgium's security, it is no longer possible to conclude alliances with other countries. Once Belgium is invaded, it must first resist alone, no matter what. The assistance measures stipulated in the alliance will only take effect after the act of aggression has occurred, which is too slow to be effective. Therefore, we must adopt a completely "Belgian" policy in the future, so that our country will not be dragged into the vortex due to disputes between neighboring countries, which is in line with the ideals of the Belgian nation. However, to implement this policy, we must make reasonable efforts in military and financial terms before it can be effective. The people of our country all have the desire to maintain peace and will definitely agree with this policy. (14th Havas Telegram)

Belgian Military Deployment 54

(Brussels) The measures decided by the State Council on military affairs yesterday focused on strengthening border defense forces, and focused on various units on the northeastern border. The seventh and eighth regiments are transferred from the central part to the northeast. The seventh regiment will be stationed in the eastern city of Tongeren (near the border of the Netherlands and Germany), the eighth regiment will be stationed in the northern city of Turnhout (near the border of the Netherlands), and another nine infantry regiments will be stationed in the city of Liège, the eastern border defense center, and the surrounding area. In addition, three infantry regiments are stationed on the southern border, one regiment is stationed in the western Flanders region, and three motorized cavalry regiments remain in the capital as support troops. (15th Havas Telegram)

Japanese Government Controls Food Supply: Joint Public-Private Organization to be Established; Rice Prices to be Regulated and Grain Production Controlled 58

(Tokyo) The Japanese Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry is planning to establish a large-scale rice control organization in Tokyo to maintain supply and manage the market. It will handle the government's rice, stockpile grains, and manage other related matters. The Ministry also proposes to abolish the existing rice exchange offices operating in nineteen major cities in Japan, and compensate the 230 licensed rice merchants for their loss of income with government funds. It is reported that after the implementation of the above two measures, the current fluctuating rice prices will cease, and speculation in rice transactions will be eliminated. This is because the rice control organization will have the power to regulate rice prices. Its capital will be jointly raised by the government and the public. In effect, this organization will represent the government in regulating rice prices and controlling grain production throughout Japan. The total amount of private investment has not yet been determined, but the total capital will be approximately 40 million yen, and the government will guarantee an annual interest of 6% to the shareholders. Details of the above plan will be announced by the Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry in the near future. (Reuters, 15th)

Japanese Ambassador to the US Speaks on Sino-Japanese Negotiations 59

The assertion that Japan has made demands that undermine Chinese sovereignty is inaccurate. However, Saito tacitly admitted that the military occupation of land is reasonable, saying that the power between individuals always waxes and wanes. Once this waxing and waning is recognized by law, society will return to peace. However, from the perspective of national defense, this transfer of power has not yet been legalized and can only be achieved through war. Therefore, condemning war is tantamount to ignoring the waxing and waning of the power of various nations and obliterating the facts. (National Telegram, 14th)

US Navy Announces: Naval Strength of Various Countries; US Ships Decrease, British and Japanese Increase 61

(Washington) The Navy Department announced today that the United States had a total of 342 warships on July 1 this year, which decreased to 306 on September 15. At the same time, Japanese warships increased from 213 to 217, and British warships increased from 307 to 309. Japan increased from 772,797 tons to 773,970 tons, and Britain increased from 1,224,329 tons to 1,232,854 tons. As for France, it built nine warships between July 1 and September 15, bringing its total to 187 warships, and its tonnage increased from 558,452 tons to 571,734 tons. (National Telegram, 14th)

Situation in North China Turns Gloomy: Important Meeting of Japanese Army in Tianjin; Diplomatic Future Appears Pessimistic 73

Tianjin Correspondence, the Chief of the Japanese Army's Special Service Agency in Shanghai, Kusonoki, arrived north on the 13th by China National Aviation Corporation plane to convey the opinions of the senior overseas leaders of the Japanese Army, Navy, and Foreign Ministry on diplomacy toward China. More than 20 people participated, including Chief of Staff Hashimoto and Senior Staff Officer Iida. Kusonoki reported on the meeting between Kawagoe and Chiang Kai-shek in Kyoto on the 9th of this month, as well as the recent diplomatic opinions decided by senior executives of the Japanese Army, Navy, and Foreign Ministry agencies in Shanghai. After lengthy discussions, the meeting adjourned at 5:00 pm due to the complexity of the relationship and the multiple parties involved, making it difficult to make a decision quickly. Another meeting is scheduled for the 16th. At that time, the generals of the Japanese Kwantung Army will send staff officers Tanaka Kichiji, Ueda, and Itagaki. After the specific plan is decided at that time, Kusonoki will bring it back to Shanghai and convey it to Kawagoe to support the progress of diplomacy. Tashiro also ordered staff officer of the Command, Wachi Takaeji, to fly to Shanghai at 1:50 pm on the 13th to visit military attachés in Shanghai such as Kita, Sasaki, and Utsunomiya to explore their intentions. On the 15th, he went to Nanjing to visit Kawagoe to inquire about the diplomatic situation. On the 16th, he rushed back to attend the meeting convened by the Japanese Kwantung and North China command headquarters in Tianjin. It is reported that before the meeting was held, Kusonoki first visited Matsumuro and Kawabe in Peiping on the 14th to discuss the matter and planned to meet with Song. On the 15th or 16th morning, he flew to Suiyuan and Chahar to meet with the chiefs of the Japanese Kwantung and North China special service agencies, Kuwabara, Omoto, Hayama, and Yokoyama, to exchange intentions. On the same day, he returned to Tianjin to attend the military attaché meeting. It is heard that the result of Kawagoe's meeting with Chiang Kai-shek on October 9 was quite pessimistic in terms of diplomacy. Originally, the hopes held by the Japanese side were difficult to achieve. The two Japanese systems stationed in China, the Army and the Navy, almost wandered on the fork of peaceful concession and decisive war. Most of the Japanese residents in Peiping and Tianjin, in view of the failure of diplomacy, published papers in the newspapers expressing that the policies adopted by the overseas agencies of the Army and Navy provinces were digging their own graves and leading their national destiny into a tragic situation. Therefore, the Japanese Army Command in North China felt a great sense of responsibility and anxiety. The scope of the meeting at the Tomishima-cho official residence in Tianjin on the 13th generally determined that the four demands on China could not be withdrawn, but they would never insist on them. The first item, the construction of a buffer zone in the five provinces of North China, would be left to the leaders of the provinces themselves to decide. The second item, Sino-Japanese economic cooperation, would be changed to start with North China first, or simply be called the economic development of North China. If there are equivalent alternative conditions for the third and fourth items, they can be withdrawn even if the quantity is lighter, so as to avoid a stalemate. It is also heard that the Japanese Kwantung and North China command headquarters are actually the basis for supporting Sino-Japanese diplomacy. At first, the two command headquarters observed the expansion of the four demands and the expansion of Japan's prestige, thinking that they could win without firing a shot. Now, they have not achieved their wishes, which is unexpected. It is still uncertain how to handle the so-called second step. At present, the talk of war seems to have passed. The collision between the two command headquarters is because the Russian side intentionally impedes the progress of Sino-Japanese diplomacy, and they have concerns. Those who initially advocated being tough to the end or advocating the use of force are now hesitant and worried about the diplomatic future. Before the Japanese side has determined its steps, the general situation in North China seems to have entered a silent stage. (14th)

The Case of Tan and Yang Accused: Full Text of the Appeal Judgment - First Instance Judgment Overturned 74

The following is the criminal judgment of the Jiangsu High Court regarding the case of Tan Zhuohong and Yang Shaopeng accused: Appellant Tan Zhuohong, male, 39 years old, resident of an apartment on Avenue Joffre, Shanghai, former judge of the Shanghai District Court, appointed defense lawyers Shan Yuhua and Yao Xiaoqiu; Appellant Yang Shaopeng, male, 48 years old, resident at No. 20, Lane 150, Baker Road, Shanghai, lawyer, appointed defense lawyers Lu Dingkui and Qian Jiazhen. The above-named appellants, dissatisfied with the first instance judgment of the Wu County District Court of the Republic of China on June 25, 1936, regarding their malfeasance case, filed an appeal. The court's judgment is as follows:

Main Text

The original judgment is reversed. Tan Zhuohong, jointly guilty of requesting bribes for actions violating his duties, is sentenced to three years and six months of imprisonment and deprivation of civil rights for four years; for abuse of authority in personally detaining someone, he is sentenced to one year of imprisonment; the sentences shall be served concurrently for a total of four years, with deprivation of civil rights for four years.

Yang Shaopeng, jointly guilty of requesting bribes for actions violating his duties, is sentenced to three years and six months of imprisonment and deprivation of civil rights for four years.

Facts

During Tan Zhuohong's tenure as a judge in the Shanghai District Court, he colluded with Yang Shaopeng, who was practicing law, to solicit bribes from litigants. In September 1935, Wu Peizhen filed a private prosecution with the Shanghai District Court against her husband, Li Keting, for the offense of interfering with marriage. Because Tan Zhuohong was handling the case, Tan Zhuohong abused his authority by detaining Li Keting. On the 9th of the same month, the court accepted Wang Bingnan and Lei Xianzhi (i.e., the law firm of Zhu Yisheng, the appointed agent for the civil lawsuit attached to the Wang Bingnan trademark counterfeiting case). Yang Shaopeng told Zhu Yisheng, "Judge Tan Zhuohong, who is handling the case, told me to tell you that if your client spends some money, the case can be handled to his satisfaction." Zhu Yisheng did not agree. Later, Zhu Yisheng relayed the incident of Yang Shaopeng soliciting a bribe to Zhao Deru, the business director of Lei Xianzhi's store. Zhao Deru also ignored it. Unexpectedly, Yang Shaopeng, still hoping there was a chance, repeatedly informed Zhu Yisheng by telephone, reducing the originally requested bribe of $2,000 to $400, and when he reduced it to $400 by phone, he stated that Tan would reopen the debate on Wang Bingnan's case, giving you one last chance," etc. Zhu Yisheng still refused. In October of the same year, Tan Zhuohong handled the private prosecution of Zhang Qidong and Yang Dingcheng against Song Dacheng for defamation. Again, using the same method, after the first trial, Yang Shaopeng, in collusion, went to Sun Zuji, the agent appointed by Zhang Qidong, et al., and stated that the evidence in the private prosecution case was weak, but if a considerable price was paid, the defendant could be severely punished. "Judge Tan sent me to contact you," and so on. Sun Zuji also did not agree. The private prosecutors Zhang Qidong, et al., having heard from Zhu Yisheng about Yang Shaopeng's solicitation of bribes, again believed it was right to refuse his request. Subsequently, the Ministry of Judicial Administration, based on a confidential report, learned that Yang Shaopeng was soliciting bribes on behalf of Tan Zhuohong and ordered an investigation and reply. It also secretly ordered the chief prosecutor of this court to transfer Tan Zhuohong, et al., to another court for investigation. After receiving the order, the chief prosecutor of this court, along with the original files, ordered the prosecutor of the Wu County District Court to investigate. As a result, Tan Zhuohong, et al., were publicly prosecuted for dereliction of duty.

Reasons

The reasons for this case are discussed separately below:

(1) Regarding the portion of Wu Peizhen's private prosecution against Li Keting, it is found that Wu Peizhen's private prosecution and the testimony provided during the first court hearing indicate that she and Li Keting have the status of a married couple. According to Article 319 of the Criminal Procedure Law, a private prosecution cannot be filed. After the appellant Tan Zhuohong took over the case, he should have directly ruled it inadmissible according to Article 326 of the same law, which would have been the proper course of action. However, he still scheduled hearings and, after questioning, ordered a security deposit of $1,000, and detained him without bail, which was not lawful. Moreover, upon investigation, Wu Peizhen's private prosecution cited Article 238 of the Criminal Law, the elements of which require a final judgment. Since the marriage between Wu Peizhen and Li Keting has not been definitively judged, it is clear that a crime has not been committed in substance. Therefore, there was no need for bail after questioning. Assuming, for the sake of argument, that the appellant's order for bail was proper, and the subsequent detention was due to lack of bail, then once bail was provided according to the court's ruling, the reason for the detention disappeared, and there was no reason to continue the detention. However, when the appellant questioned the guarantor on the 15th, he demanded that the guarantor also be responsible for the attached civil lawsuit of $10,000, which can only be described as absurd. If we further assume that Wu Peizhen's attached civil lawsuit was filed after the court ordered bail, then the appellant's demand that the guarantor also guarantee the amount claimed in the attached civil lawsuit outside of the court's ruling could be justified. However, the investigation of the files reveals that Wu Peizhen's attached civil lawsuit of $10,000 was stated in the private prosecution document, and should have been examined by the appellant before the court ruling. Tan Zhuohong granted bail to Li Keting clearly because of the criminal matter, not for the attached civil lawsuit. Now, despite the guarantor's willingness to bear the $1,000 security deposit as per the court's ruling, he unreasonably demanded that the guarantor guarantee the amount claimed in the attached civil lawsuit. When the guarantor refused, he stated that he would allow the guarantor to consider and then question him again, thus continuing Li Keting's detention. His crime of abuse of power by detention is truly undeniable. In this regard, the appellant argued, "At that time, I only told the guarantor that there was an attached civil lawsuit of $10,000, but I did not want the guarantor to guarantee the attached civil lawsuit. The part about the guarantor guaranteeing it in the record is a mistake," etc. However, the record in question has been signed by the appellant, making it difficult to deny it as a record error. As evidenced by the fact that Li Keting's defense lawyer, Lu Jianai, appeared in court on the 17th of the same month, the appellant questioned him whether he was willing to guarantee the attached civil lawsuit of $10,000 in Wu Peizhen's lawsuit against Li Keting for marriage fraud, and only after he answered yes was Li Keting released. Therefore, there is no doubt that the words "the guarantor guarantees the attached civil lawsuit" in the record are not a mistake. Further investigation reveals that after Li Keting was detained, Yang Shaopeng went to Gao Junxiang's (i.e., Li Keting's defense lawyer) office. He described what Judge Tan asked you what your opinion of this case was, and Lu Jianai at the time described, I have an opinion, a spouse cannot privately prosecute, Judge Tan's illegal detention is wrong, please tell Judge Tan not to violate the law, etc., according to Gao Junxiang and Lu Jianai's consistent testimony. The appellant Yang Shaopeng not only clearly admitted at the time how Lu Jianai pointed out Tan Zhuohong's violation of the law, but also said, "I therefore called Tan Zhuohong, please refer to the law together, and handle it carefully." Tan Zhuohong also stated in the original trial, "I was harmed by your (referring to Yang Shaopeng) phone call," etc. It is the appellant Tan Zhuohong who first detained Li Keting abusively, intending to facilitate the solicitation of bribes, and then, when Lu Jianai pointed out his illegality, fearing disaster, voluntarily changed the original court ruling and did not allow him to provide bail, and directly handed Li Keting over to Lu Jianai, hoping to avoid responsibility. This is even more certain. The original trial was not improper in finding Tan Zhuohong guilty of abuse of power by detention in this part. The crime in Article 128 of the Criminal Law refers to the situation where a civil servant accepts a lawsuit that they have no right to accept. Wu Peizhen's private prosecution should be accepted by the court, but the application of the private prosecution procedure is inappropriate. The court should make a judgment of inadmissibility, which is different from the crime stipulated in the above-mentioned legal text. The original trial also found Tan Zhuohong guilty of this crime, but their opinion is not quite appropriate. Furthermore, the crime of soliciting bribes requires that the intention of soliciting has reached the other party or their appointed agent before it can be established. Otherwise, even if there is a soliciting act, it is still an attempt, and there is no explicit provision for punishment in the law. In this case, although the appellants colluded to solicit bribes, Yang Shaopeng only expressed the intention of soliciting bribes to Gao Junxiang, Li Keting's defense lawyer (according to Gao Junxiang, Yang Shaopeng asked what opinions he had, but he didn't explicitly mention money). This intention did not reach the detained Li Keting, so it is still an attempted solicitation. The original trial believed that the appellants were also guilty of soliciting bribes in this part, which is unfair and should be reversed and re-judged by this court.

(2) Regarding the Wang Bingnan counterfeiting trademark case and the Zhang Qidong et al. private prosecution of Song Dacheng for defamation cases, the investigation reveals that the appellant Tan Zhuohong handled the Wang Bingnan and Song Dacheng cases in October of last year. After the first hearing in each case, Yang Shaopeng went to Zhu Yisheng and Sun Zuji's law firms successively. He told Zhu Yisheng that Judge Tan told me to tell you to spend some money, and the case can be handled to his satisfaction. He continued to notify Zhu Yi by phone, instructing him to pay $2,000, and when Zhu Yi refused, he reduced it to $1,000, and finally to $400. He said when reducing to $400 that the case has been reopened for debate, and there is an undecided opportunity for you in court. He told Sun Zuji that the evidence in Zhang Qidong's private prosecution case was weak. Judge Tan told me to contact you. If a considerable price is paid, the defendant can be severely punished, etc. Zhu Yisheng and Sun Zuji pointed this out in detail as if they were describing a painting. Sun Zuji's statement that Yang Shaopeng said that the debate would be reopened is consistent with the record. That is, the appellant Yang Shaopeng did not deny that he went to Zhu Yisheng and Sun Zuji's law firms to discuss the cases. His defense was that he did not go to Zhu and Sun's firms on his own initiative, but that Zhu and Sun had called him by phone one after another, asking him to intercede with Judge Tan. Tan Zhuohong's main defense was that I did not know Yang Shaopeng, and Sun Zuji and Zhu Yisheng said that he would judge their cases and solicit bribes in my name. This is just Yang Shaopeng's behavior. How can it be considered my behavior? Not to mention that Yang Shaopeng does not admit this behavior, even if he did have this kind of behavior, it was just him using my name to swindle and deceive others, and it cannot be attributed to me, etc. However, Zhao Deru testified, "After this case was prosecuted, the criminal court held a hearing once. I went to Zhu Yisheng's place to inquire about the situation. Zhu Yisheng said that Yang Shaopeng came and told us to spend some money in court. We didn't pay attention because the evidence was solid." Zhang Qidong testified, "This case had a first hearing on October 14th last year. I went to Sun's law firm outside of the 10th and said, on the 16th of this month, lawyer Yang Shaopeng came to negotiate this case and said that he was Judge Tan who was handling the case in court, and asked him to say that our case's evidence was weak. If we want to convict the defendant, we must have a considerable price. At the time, I refused, etc. I said at the time that the refusal was correct." Yang Dingcheng's testimony was roughly the same. Furthermore, according to the testimony of Chen Fengming and Wang Jiacheng, after Yang Shaopeng met with Sun Zuji, Sun Zuji came back and said as a joke that to handle a small case, the judge in the court told him that my evidence was weak. To convict the defendant, I must pay a considerable price, etc., which is consistent with Zhu Yisheng and Sun Zuji's statements. This is sufficient proof that Zhu Yisheng and Sun Zuji's statements are credible. Therefore, the fact that the appellants solicited bribes can be confirmed. Moreover, the investigation reveals that Yang Shaopeng wrote to his wife, Chen Qinbao, from the detention center, stating, "I usually never received any money at home or on my person." "Thief Tan now wants to say some things that he shouldn't say, he wants to bite me and accuse me of fraud. My only evidence is the photo mentioned above. Sister Qingqin, be careful, be sure to hand the photo and the negative to Shen Xianniu for safekeeping. If Thief Tan harms me, I will use it as evidence, and Thief Tan will be in trouble. But don't show it now. Also, when the official asked for Mr. Chen Hanshi's address, I pretended to only know Shanjia Garden, and not the lane number. Now Chen has gone to Tianjin and Beiping. In case they find out Chen Hanshi's address and want to summon Mr. Chen, ask both teachers' wives to be sure to say that they don't know anything about men's affairs. Women don't know anything at all. (Omission) If Tan's family and lawyer Yang and I, as men, had any contact with Mr. Chen, force him to confess." "This letter must not be kept at home, nor should it be torn up. It can be given to Brother Shen to keep at his mansion." He also wrote to Zhang Shizhao, stating, "If I didn't uphold justice, he (referring to Tan Zhuohong) would really be in trouble. The reason for his usual behavior is hard to put into words," etc. Although the photo in question has not been seized, and Yang Shaopeng and his wife Chen Qinbao are unwilling to produce it, based on the above text, Yang Shaopeng's solicitation of bribes for Tan Zhuohong and the fact that his solicitation was not baseless, and that the fact of collusion to solicit bribes was known to Chen Hanshi's wife, et al., are ultimately obvious. Considering that Yang Shaopeng immediately notified Tan Zhuohong by phone after Lu Jia Ding pointed out Tan Zhuohong's illegal handling of the Li Keting case, asking him to refer to the law, and that Yang Shaopeng's home had Tan Zhuohong's business card, and Yang Shaopeng's letter mentioned that there was an invitation from Tan Zhuohong to a dinner at Da Jiali in his office drawer, the daily collusion between the appellants is even clearer. Tan Zhuohong's defense that he did not know Yang Shaopeng is an attempt to cover up the truth. The defense, etc., is all fabricated to avoid responsibility and cannot be believed. The original trial was not improper in finding that the appellants continuously solicited bribes in these parts. However, the crime of divulging secrets in Article 132 of the Criminal Law refers to the situation of divulging matters that should be kept secret. If a lawsuit is reopened for debate, it should be stated publicly that there is no so-called secret. When the appellant was soliciting a bribe in the Wang Bingnan case at the end, he claimed that the debate was reopened, giving you an undecided opportunity, just delaying the time to achieve the purpose of soliciting bribes. It is difficult to recognize that he also committed the crime of divulging secrets. Although the original trial found that the rules applied by the appellant in the Wang Bingnan case were not inappropriate, the original judgment sentenced the appellant for continuous offenses. Since other parts of the appellant have reasons for reversal, this part is ultimately unsustainable. (To be continued)

Songjiang 75

Scheduled Widening of Changqiao Street

Since the opening of the motor road in this city, the Changqiao Street outside the west gate has been the most convenient for connecting to the motor road and is located in the center of the West Gate Main Street. Therefore, entertainment businesses such as theaters are located here. The market on Changqiao Street has been growing year by year. However, the street is extremely narrow, and there is a risk of danger when two vehicles meet. The county government's 52nd meeting decided to widen the street, stipulating a width of 12 meters, with sidewalks of 1 meter on each side. The buildings on both sides should be taken into account. The existing road surface should be measured and a plan drawn up, which should be submitted to the finance and construction departments for instructions. It is now scheduled to start construction on February 15. The buildings on both sides of the street must be demolished and taken in accordance with the plan before December 5.

Nanhui 76

Theatrical Bandits Kill and Rob

About two miles outside the west gate of this county, in Baojia Township, District 1, farmer Yin Xingeng, who started by carrying water, built nine tile-roofed houses, which were coveted by bandits. At about 11 o'clock the night before, about 20 bandits broke into the side door. His son, Xilou, immediately went up to the roof and blew a whistle, which caused the bandits to fire at the roof, hitting his left leg and abdomen with six or seven shots. His son, Juezi, who was hanging upstairs, was also hit by stray bullets, injuring his forehead and hand. At this time, the neighbors were awakened and the sound of people was loud, and the bandits did not dare to rob and fled north after sounding their whistles. Xilou died of serious injuries. According to Yin Xingeng's family, six or seven of the bandits were wearing uniforms, leggings, and holding five or six long and short guns. Yesterday, the county Public Security Bureau sent personnel to investigate and reported it to the county government, which ordered the arrest. In addition, the home of Cao Chuanlin, a farmer in Zao Hong, District 1, was also robbed of more than 20 packages of cotton and more than 10 pieces of homespun cloth by more than a dozen bandits a few days ago. The servant Ni Xue was tied up with ropes and beaten, causing serious injuries. Yesterday, he was also carried to the county to have his injuries examined and request an investigation.

Wuxi 77

Promotion of Mechanical Silk Filatures

Since the Construction Department implemented the sericulture control, everything has gradually gotten on track. The price of silkworm eggs, the guidance of sericulture technology, and the cultivation of mulberry seedlings have all made considerable progress in recent years. However, the silk filatures have not been improved and are still old-fashioned silk kilns. They must be roasted by manpower, which increases costs and makes the quality of the goods uneven, which greatly affects the length of the silk. Currently, the cost of drying silkworm cocoons is about one yuan, which is unfavorable to farmers and silk merchants. If mechanical kilns are used, the cost of drying will be reduced, and each load will only cost about six or seven yuan. Currently, only Jintan County in Jiangsu Province uses mechanical kilns. In this county, Sitou Gongtailong silk filature also has a facility. However, the equipment cost is quite large, and official-merchant cooperation is required for investment and transformation. The Jiangsu Construction Department plans to gradually promote it starting in the spring of next year and must complete it within three years.

Changshu 78

Rural Teachers Transformed into Agricultural Professionals

The rural normal school in Xitangqiao had all of its students graduate this summer, and the department ordered the school to be closed. It has repeatedly requested to continue, but has not been approved. This school was founded in 1932 and has already reached a certain scale, so it is a pity to close it suddenly. Currently, people in the education field, because schools are developed in the territory, but senior high schools are still lacking, have jointly petitioned to run an agricultural vocational high school so that ordinary children can have the opportunity to continue their education. The Department of Education believes that an agricultural vocational high school can indeed remedy the education in Changshu, and has approved it and instructed the Education Bureau to start preparing, and it is expected to be realized in the next semester.

Large Batch of Banknotes Consumed in Flames

Shen Fugeng, a farmer from Sanliqiao, Nantang outside the east gate, came to the city yesterday with his son in a boat to sell rice, totaling 18 shi of white rice, which was sold for 144 yuan in legal tender. After receiving the money, he planned to return home, but feeling hungry, Shen went ashore to have some noodles cooked. Fearing loss, he handed the money over to his son, strictly ordering him not to go ashore to prevent pickpocketing. Unexpectedly, his son saw that his father had been waiting for a long time and was not coming back, so he secretly hid the banknotes in the stove to prevent any problems. He then went ashore to find his father, but did not meet him. Unexpectedly, when he returned to the boat, he saw that his father had already returned and was lighting a fire to cook noodles. His son was shocked and called out, telling him that there were banknotes hidden in the stove. They quickly put out the fire and searched, but the 144 yuan in banknotes had been reduced to ashes. At that time, Shen's nerves went haywire, and all who saw it were greatly grieved.

Wei came to the department on the 13th for screening and was detained. He has now been ordered to send personnel from the district to the province to bring him back to the case and interrogate him according to law.

A Chinese driver was driving through Babao, Haining, when the foreign driver took over. Due to excessive speed, the car suddenly fell into a pond. The driver has been sent to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Jiangsu Shanghai First Special District Court 8559 Public Notice (Application for Guardianship of Yu Jianyuan's Estate) 83

Public Notice: Yu Huding and Zhang Zhao filed an application for the issuance of a certificate of guardianship of estate, stating that the late husband and late father, Yu Jianyuan, a native of Wuyuan, Anhui, died on August 27, 1933, leaving 11 shares of Union Insurance Society of Canton Limited, numbered from 78011 to 78020 and from 90728 to 90729. According to law, the applicants should inherit the management and operation of the property. They requested that the court approve the issuance of a certificate of guardianship of estate for the purpose of transfer, etc. Therefore, a public notice is issued in the newspaper for general knowledge. If anyone has any objections to this application, they must come to the court to state their objections within 20 days from the date of publication until the publication is stopped. If no one states any objections after the deadline, the court will issue a certificate of guardianship of estate.
