Special Telecommunications Issue

The Significance of Sending Telegrams to Celebrate a Birthday 196

— Zhen

According to newspapers, the birthday of Executive Yuan President Chiang Kai-shek is October 29th of the Gregorian calendar. This year marks his 50th birthday. The President advocates a frugality campaign, so this event should not be extravagant. Officials of various agencies will only send letters or telegrams of congratulations on that day and will not send gifts, it is said. President Chiang has a firm foundation and embraces humility. He is a shining example, and those who hear of it can agree with it.

President Chiang is the leader of the Party and the country, and his hard work is highly meritorious. The people of the whole country have long wanted to purchase airplanes to celebrate his birthday while warmly supporting him. This matter is related to national defense and should be discussed separately. As for giving gifts, since an instruction to stop has been issued, it should be followed. However, if officials of various agencies and the people of the whole country only send letters or telegrams of congratulations on that day, given the vastness of our country's territory and the time required for postal delivery, there is a risk that the time will be insufficient or overdue. The only way to remedy this is to send social telegrams.

The use of social telegrams is not limited to one purpose, but its significance is actually imitating the international practice of sending congratulatory telegrams. Looking at the people of Europe and America, whenever the birthday of the head of state is celebrated, they all send congratulatory telegrams to express their congratulations. On that day, the telegraph bureau works overtime and is busy. Congratulatory telegrams from all directions fly in like snowflakes, and the enthusiastic atmosphere is enough to see one aspect. The Ministry of Transportation initiated social telegrams and set the price at a particularly low level to facilitate public communication. It is the most appropriate celebration method.

Moreover, President Chiang's service to the country is far above that of the heads of state of other countries. All of our people should send a social congratulatory telegram on that day, regardless of distance, whether individual or group, to express their sincerity in support, to promote the way of frugality, and to be economical in time, simple in procedures, solemn in meaning, and novel in method. All telegraph offices in the country can send telegrams. Patriotic people will surely be happy to adopt it.

Necessary Conditions for Success of International Traders 197

— Yuan Ming

To compete in the ever-changing international business arena and to stand out, one must possess exceptional vision, unwavering determination, and skillful maneuvering. However, "being well-informed" is ultimately a key element for success. Matters such as market price fluctuations, source conditions, sluggish or booming sales, etc., must be known quickly and thoroughly. Only then can strategies be decided and opportunities be seized promptly. Otherwise, even a slight delay will allow others to get ahead. Therefore, the speed of information can determine success or failure in the business world. To be well-informed, the effective use of communication tools is crucial—that is, after obtaining commercial information, using the fastest communication methods to transmit it. Currently, the fastest international communication method is the "telegram." However, there are many telegraph circuits with varying speeds. Therefore, when using telegrams for communication, one must also understand how to choose the right circuit. The fastest and best telegraph circuit from China to the rest of the world right now is the "International Wireless Circuit"—"fast" is the objective for selecting a circuit, and "good" includes attentive service and providing various conveniences to the public.

Why is the International Wireless Telegraph the fastest and most advantageous? Because it communicates directly with major cities in various countries, using the latest high-speed equipment, making it incomparably "fast." Furthermore, constant attention is paid to improving internal operations. Two points are particularly noteworthy: (1) Strict Proofreading—the accuracy of the telegram text is of utmost importance. Therefore, the international radio station has specially assigned trained personnel to handle proofreading. Each telegram is proofread immediately after receipt or transmission. If there are any errors, they are notified and corrected immediately without waiting for the recipient to inquire. This is of great benefit to both senders and receivers because waiting for the sender or receiver to discover the error and then inquire would inevitably cause delays. As a result of implementing this, telegrams are extremely accurate and error-free. (2) Increasing Retransmission Speed—the Shanghai Telegraph Office originally had a dedicated line for the international radio station to relay telegrams from various domestic locations to foreign countries. Later, to further increase speed, multiple multiplex machines were installed, enabling international telegrams from major bureaus to be transmitted directly to the international radio station. Since the implementation of this measure, the speed of telegram transmission has increased significantly! In addition, measures such as restricting the delivery time of messengers and implementing telephone transmission of telegrams are all related to increasing telegram speed.

Therefore, for commercial firms engaged in international trade, if they send international telegrams, they only need to specify "via wireless" or "Via Cgra" to receive complete satisfaction. Those commercial firms that have already adopted international wireless telegrams have practically experienced various conveniences and will undoubtedly believe my words are true. Those commercial firms that have not yet adopted international wireless telegrams, but definitely hope for swift telegram transmission, may well experiment to see if what I say is true. Moreover, international wireless is a newly established state-owned enterprise in our country. All our citizens should support and adopt it to further its development, especially since the rewards it offers are exceptionally swift and include attentive service and various conveniences.

We know that the more developed the communication industry, the more communication efficiency can be improved; the more convenient communication methods become, the more they can promote the prosperity of international trade. Therefore, international traders, for the sake of their businesses and for the sake of patriotism, cannot but think big and unanimously support this emerging state-owned enterprise, cooperating closely with the telegraph bureau to jointly promote the economic revival of the nation.

Issues Regarding International Telegram Rates 198

— Bao Zhen

The formulation of international telegram rates is quite complex. International telegram rates vary among countries, with significant discrepancies. Some distances are the same but prices differ greatly; some gold franc prices are similar, but the values of various countries' conversions to their own currencies vary widely. It is difficult to generalize. The current international telegram rates in our country are not entirely based on distance, but distance remains an important factor in determining international telegram rates.

Due to historical reasons, various countries calculate international telegram distances based on the length of the wire route, not the spatial distance. For example, the telegraph line from our country to the United States passes through the Philippines or Japan, so the price between China and the United States should be higher than the price between the Philippines and the United States or between Japan and the United States. This time, organizations such as the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce compared the spatial distance and price from Little Luzon to the United States, and from Japan to the United States, with the spatial distance and price from China to the United States, and hastily concluded that the price between China and the United States was higher. This is actually due to a lack of understanding of the aforementioned principle. Furthermore, Little Luzon is only a port in the Philippine Islands, and Japan is only one of the many countries in the Far East. If one wants to compare the telegram price from China to the United States with those from other countries to the United States, it seems appropriate to compare the prices from various important countries in the Far East to the United States in order to understand the whole picture. A table is listed below for comparison:

Origin-Destination　Longitude　Price in Gold Francs　Comparison with China-US Price

China——San Francisco　3.75

Hong Kong——San Francisco (British territory)　3.75　Equal

Macau——San Francisco (Portuguese territory)　4.15　Higher by 0.40

Vietnam——San Francisco　3.99　Higher by 0.24

Federated Malay States and Straits Settlements——San Francisco　4.35　Higher by 0.60

——San Francisco　3.75　Equal

East Indies——San Francisco　4.35　Higher by 0.60

India——San Francisco　3.25　Lower by 0.50

Japan——San Francisco　3.05　Lower by 0.70

Philippines——San Francisco

From Little Luzon　2.65　Lower by 1.10

From Luzon Island　2.90　Lower by 0.85

From other islands　3.55　Lower by 0.20

(Note: The basic price for telegrams sent from various countries to China is based on those sent to Shanghai. Those sent to other locations outside Shanghai require additional inland fees. The basic price for telegrams sent from various countries to the United States is based on those sent to San Francisco. Other locations outside San Francisco also require additional line fees. Therefore, the above table uses telegrams sent to San Francisco as the standard.)

From the above table, it can be seen that the prices of telegrams from various countries in the Far East to the United States are sometimes equal to those from China to the United States, sometimes higher than those from China, and sometimes lower than those from China. The telegram price between China and the United States cannot be said to be uniquely expensive. Furthermore, the Ministry of Communications of our country has signed service contracts with the American Wireless Transportation Company, Great Eastern, Great Northern, and other telegraph companies regarding matters such as telegram transmission and fee collection, which are to be jointly observed. Although any party can propose discussions regarding increases or decreases in telegram prices, the other party's agreement will still depend on whether the reasons are sufficient and whether the facts require detailed consideration and negotiation to decide.

The so-called attempt by the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, the Sino-American Trade Association, and other four organizations to send a telegram of one hundred words from Shanghai to San Francisco, and then have the original telegram sent back from San Francisco to Shanghai, during which the Shanghai side must pay more than one hundred and ten yuan in Chinese currency, indicating that our country's international telegram exchange rate is also more expensive, is actually not entirely true. The price in gold francs for telegrams between China and the United States is originally equal on both sides. The above difference is actually due to the special monetary policy adopted by the United States. Therefore, the power to adjust the above difference rests with the United States and not with our country. According to the current situation, the lower the value of the US dollar or the higher the world silver price, the greater the difference between the amount of national currency paid in China and the equivalent amount of national currency paid in the United States for telegrams between China and the United States. Now that the Yellow Kingdom has adopted a special monetary policy and also holds the authority to manipulate world silver prices, future trends may increase the above difference. For example, according to the current legal exchange rate in our country, if our country wants to equalize the national currency values of the China-US prices, it must reduce the current gold franc conversion rate by about 41% (i.e., each gold franc equals 67 cents). However, the US Silver Purchase Act stipulates that the silver price may be raised to one dollar and twenty-nine cents (USD) per ounce (currently only worth about 45 cents). If this matter is realized and our country's legal exchange rate can still remain unchanged, then our country's gold franc conversion rate must be reduced by 79% of the current rate (each gold franc equals 23.5 cents) to equalize the national currency values of the China-US prices. If the United States further devalues ​​its currency in the future, then our country's gold franc conversion rate must be reduced again. Would this not make our country's gold franc conversion rate not based on China's legal exchange rate, but instead shift with the monetary policy of the United States? In short, the current gold franc conversion rate in the United States is not equal to the true value of the gold franc; this is what is meant by special monetary policy. If this special monetary policy is not changed, it is feared that all telegrams between the world's countries and the United States will not take into account fees, so the national currency price rate converted from the set gold franc cannot only be applied to telegrams sent to a certain country or a certain circuit. If our country reduces the gold franc conversion rate, then the national currency prices for telegrams sent to all countries in the world must be reduced across the board. However, our country's payment to various foreign telegraph companies (wireless or submarine) for fees, due to the restrictions of the International Telegraph Convention and the service contracts signed between our country and various countries, must still be calculated at the full value of the gold franc. If this is done, our country's telecommunications economics will suffer significant losses, which is hardly permissible with current financial resources.

The more developed international trade is, the more international telegrams there will be; this is a certain principle. At the same time, international telegrams are a necessary communication tool for conducting international trade. Therefore, although reducing telegram prices can promote international trade, it is difficult to determine this strength. Let me explain as follows: If international trade between China and the United States increases by 50%, then telegram business may increase by 50%. If the price between China and the United States is reduced by 50%, then between China and the United States...

Although our country's telegram service is a state-owned enterprise, it has no state treasury subsidy, so it must take into account the balance of income and expenditure in terms of economics. Assuming that after the price between China and the United States is reduced by 50%, trade between China and the United States can also increase by 50%, thus increasing the return telegram business between China and the United States by 50%. Although the price is reduced, the telegram fee income may not be reduced too much as a result of business development. However, since the effect of reducing international telegram prices on promoting international trade is difficult to determine, it is impossible to be sure how much telegram business can increase. Our country's international telegram fee income will inevitably be greatly reduced, not only increasing the difficulty of our country's telecommunications economics, but also being difficult for various foreign submarine cable telegraph and wireless telegraph companies to agree to.

Based on the above reasons, our country's current gold franc conversion rate is close to the gold franc exchange rate, so there is no need to change it easily at the moment, and the international telegram price is also difficult to reduce suddenly. The reason is very clear and should be understood by all sectors.

Disputes in the Huazhong Games 214

— Jianping

We have seen reports on the grand opening of the games for the four provinces of Huazhong (Anhui, Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi). Regrettably, we have also seen reports of disputes, which seem to occur at every sports event. The Hubei team refused to accept the decision and injured Huang Yuanshu, a competitor from Anhui, and disrupted the competition. Eventually, He Jian, Chairman of Hunan Province, mediated, and the Hubei team took responsibility, apologized to the Anhui team, and punished the offenders.

Although this dispute was peacefully resolved quickly, we have seen the secrets of the field. This proves that our star system hinders athleticism. After athletes came back from Berlin with "duck eggs," this is another good lesson and answer to the star system.

We will analyze this conflict.

Such disputes are common in every event. Athletes violate the principles and lose rationality. Arriving late and getting disqualified is fair, and there is no reason not to accept it. If you disagree, you make a written complaint to the committee. Not knowing the rules can be forgiven, but disrupting order and even injuring athletes is unforgivable. It should be noted that Huang Yuanshu won the 10,000-meter race (according to news from Changsha on the 12th), proving the lack of rationality of the Hubei athletes. This should be severely punished.

We cannot place the full blame on the athletes. While athletes make irrational moves, their leaders and the system that encourages them, the star system, should take part of the blame. It will take a while to spread athletics to the masses. But looking at these senseless disputes, we cannot defend the star system.

If athleticism is narrowly for a few outstanding individuals to win on behalf of groups, schools, or nations, then Chinese athleticism is like bullfighting, just for entertainment and creating disputes.

Visit to the Gaoqiao Rural Improvement Association 215

— Xishan

(Special Dispatch from this Newspaper) In recent years, the call for rural improvement has spread across the country, but most practical methods and specific steps are still in the pilot stage. The Rural Improvement Association in Gaoqiao District of this city has already begun implementation. The purpose of its organization is to build a healthy unit with an autonomous organization, which, under the guidance of the municipal government, will become the most exemplary rural area in the city. It has been three years since its establishment. When it was first established, the late General Manager Mr. Shi Liangcai also provided great help to the association. Yesterday, I paid a special visit to the association. Mr. Zhang, the manager, received me and described in detail the internal organization and implementation of the work of the association:

The area served by the Improvement Association includes Gaoqiao and Gaoxing districts, totaling 338 villages and 6,683 households. The scope of work for the people in the two districts includes agriculture, animal husbandry, and fishery. Therefore, the organization of the association is also quite extensive, proceeding in several aspects: (1) economy, (2) autonomy, (3) education, (4) hygiene, (5) agricultural affairs, and (6) crafts. There are dozens of service personnel, distributed in various districts, with Mr. Wang Kuizheng as the general manager. When it was first established, the funds were donated by local public-spirited individuals. Later, the regular expenses were stipulated to be 700 yuan per month for the first phase, 550 yuan for the second phase, and 400 yuan for the third phase, including salaries, food, and office expenses. Currently, it has reached the second phase, so the regular expenses have been reduced to 550 yuan per month. According to Mr. Zhang, although the expenses are limited by funds and cannot be abundant, they are still manageable according to the budget.

In terms of rural economic administration, the association has organized production mutual aid societies and cooperatives: (1) The establishment of production mutual aid societies aims to alleviate the economic panic of farmers, so that farmers will not stop production due to lack of capital. In terms of loan funds, it cooperates with the Agricultural Department of the Shanghai Bank. A total of 32 societies are set up in the general association and sub-districts. Each group of mutual aid members has at least five people and is jointly and severally liable for repayment. The use and amount of loans are subject to extremely strict investigation, and the standard is to meet the minimum needs of the borrowers. According to Mr. Zhang, for example, if planting five mu of land requires 1.5 yuan per mu for fertilization and 1 yuan for labor, then a loan of 10 yuan will be given. In terms of procedures, the borrower must first apply for registration, and then staff will be dispatched to investigate. If there is no fraud, the loan will be given. (2) The organization of cooperatives includes cooperative marketing of products and purchase of agricultural supplies, as well as the promotion of high-quality cotton seeds. It has cooperated with the Yangsi Cotton Field of the Central University to promote 2,500 kilograms of Jiangyin white seed cotton, and the results are good.

In terms of autonomy, the association divides the improved area into nine sub-districts to carry out the autonomous organization of the sub-districts. In terms of the people, in addition to the security corps and amateur military training classes, each branch association also generates a youth service corps. The organizational plan is divided into three phases. The first is the liaison phase, the second is the training phase, including literacy research, vocational guidance, academic lectures, and security training, and the last is the service phase. The service scope currently underway includes literacy schools, health propaganda, and home economics improvement.

The association's work in education is also quite complete. Yide Elementary School is established in Xinkangzhai, Gaoqiao, and all educational work is centered on this as a concentrated promotion point. The working situation is divided into: (1) A public library with more than 2,000 books and more than 1,005 magazines. The library is equipped with book inserts, mobile libraries, and educational outreach vehicles. It is also accompanied by displays of agricultural specimens for the public to browse. (2) Men's night school, located at the association's Xinkang office. According to reports, the students' level has reached above the third or fourth grade of elementary school, so they are now taught writing letters, abacus, English and other courses. (3) Women's night school, located in Yide Elementary School, is hosted by female staff in the area. There are 70 students, and the textbook is the literacy textbook for the common people issued by Shanghai City. (4) Running a small teacher training class to teach literacy in various houses in the district has now ended. There are more than a dozen small teachers who have graduated. (5) Appointed nine tea gardens to compile and post public wall newspapers, including three items: international, domestic, and local news. I went to visit a tea garden near Xijie and saw that the news collected on the wall newspaper was concise and clear, and the font was neat and large, which was very convenient for reading. There was also an inquiry and writing service attached to the place to reduce the difficulty of farmers in terms of writing.

The implementation work of agricultural affairs is that the association designated special contracted farmland to cooperate with farmers, giving them excellent varieties and guiding them in cultivation methods, so that farmers can obtain satisfactory harvests, and hold agricultural exhibitions from time to time to collect specimens and hanging pictures, using various citation methods to promote farmers' improvement and research. Mr. Zhang also mentioned that he had previously established a demonstration farm to plant wheat, green vegetables, and olives to test whether they were suitable for planting in the local soil. The trial has now been completed, and what is currently underway is to prepare for the establishment of a rural cotton ginning factory and a water-lifting cooperative.

The health work in the improved area is assisted by the Gaoqiao Health Office. In addition to investigating the general situation of deaths and diseases, farmers are educated on household cleaning and hygiene knowledge. In medical affairs, a public clinic is established to provide free diagnosis and treatment for farmers, and health and anti-drug campaigns are held from time to time.

The craft training includes women's embroidery classes. In Gaoqiao, women's embroidery is the main sideline, but the technology is too bad, so the works are too bad, and no one cares about them. Therefore, the association specially opened classes for training and tried to improve them. It is said that there are more than 40 graduates in the first session. Secondly, a rural craft society was established. In recent years, the city has been depressed, and industry and commerce have failed. Rural youths have no way out. Under this situation, the association has also promoted rural crafts, directed by Shi, and enrolled students to practice for six months to graduate. The initial products are rattan.

Fugitive 218

— Meiping

The moon hung like a sickle in the west of the sky, with no stars. The watchtower had already sounded the fifth watch. In this biting cold dawn, a black shadow suddenly shot across the city wall like an arrow. The watchtower sentry occasionally looked up and glanced at it, but the black shadow had agilely climbed over the city teeth, like a monkey, somersaulting and escaping over the high city wall, and falling into the grass pile at the foot of the wall.

This place is already near Beiguan. It is a wilderness with no people. Thorns and weeds are as high as sorghum stalks, taller than half a person. The black shadow crouched and used both hands as oars to break the weeds in front of him. He was in such a hurry that he didn't care about the skin on his hands, feet, or body being pierced by thorns, or perhaps already dripping with blood. He wanted to escape this wilderness in the shortest possible time and reach the pier outside Beiguan. There are small steamers heading east, west, north, and south on the pier. As long as he catches a boat, he will be a free body. (To be continued)

Movies

The Long-Awaited War Film "Serve the Country Faithfully" to Be Released 229

Twentieth Century Fox has put all its efforts this year into filming "Serve the Country Faithfully," also known as Road to Glory, setting a new record in the history of war films. Just consider the three main actors in the film: Frederic March, Warner Baxter, and Lionel Barrymore. These three stars are all capable of carrying a film on their own. Now that they are acting together in one film, it is naturally even more worth seeing. In addition, the director of this film, Howard Hawks, is a leading figure specializing in war films. Therefore, the war scenes in this film are even more intense than "All Quiet on the Western Front." It is said that Chinese leader President Chiang Kai-shek, admiring the film's reputation, had it specially transported to Lushan to watch it himself. The film will soon be released in Shanghai.

Robert Taylor and Barbara Stanwyck Co-Star in "His Brother's Wife"

Showing in Nanjing

Aviation Film "China Clipper" 230

Showing at the Grand Theater Tonight

Warner Bros.' latest historical aviation blockbuster, "China Clipper," is scheduled to be shown at the Grand Theater starting at 7:15 PM tonight (Friday). The film stars a dozen major stars, including Pat O'Brien, Beverly Roberts, and Ross Alexander. It depicts the brave and sacrificial spirit of a group of aviation pioneers, who risk their lives in stormy skies to fulfill their ambitions. The story is based on the long-distance flight of the "China Clipper" on the Pan American route not long ago, which started from Alameda on the Pacific coast near San Francisco and ended in the Philippine Islands. The film's purpose is to encourage the spirit of adventure and stimulate progressive thinking. The tense and exciting performances are even more commendable, especially at a time when we are shouting "Aviation to Save the Country." Everyone should appreciate this film.

Regarding "Happiness is Coming" 231

The two films directed by Yue Feng, "Happiness is Coming" and "Auspicious Patterns," have both been completed one after another. It is said that after "Little Sisters," Xinguang will show "Happiness is Coming."

"Happiness is Coming" stars Zhou Xuan, Ma Luofen, Guan Hongda, Qin Tong, Zhao Jingna, Liang Dusheng, and other major stars. The plot of the play takes exposing the inside story of a large family as its theme, and is full of humorous and funny gags. All dozens of scenes will make you laugh until your stomach hurts and tears come to your eyes.

The script for "Happiness is Coming" was written by Huang Jiamo. According to Huang, the play depicts the extravagance and depravity of wealthy families in rural villages, doing all kinds of evil. In particular, the lecherous old men covet the village girls, using all sorts of tricks, and making countless jokes. It truly combines satire, humor, and slapstick in one. I don't believe that anyone who watches this play won't laugh wildly.

Zhou Xuan was borrowed by Xinhua to star in "Carnival Night," which received great praise. This time, her performance in "Happiness is Coming" is even more brilliant. She plays a bride who is robbed halfway. Later, she hides in a coffin and suffocates the wealthy and unkind old man to death. It is truly full of twists and turns, and makes people's imagination run wild. The mystery in this cannot be broken until it is seen at the public screening.
